**–ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞:** –°–µ–π—á–∞—Å –µ—Å—Ç—å –¥—É–±–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ ‚Äî `init-project.sh` –ª–µ–∂–∏—Ç –∏ –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–Ω–µ —Ä–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è, –∏ –≤ `dist-release/`. –ü–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å —Å–∫–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∏–∑ –∫–æ—Ä–Ω—è (—á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ GitHub UI), –∞ `dist-release/` –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–ª—è GitHub Releases.

### üë§ **User** *(09.12.2025, 23:58)*

In general, we have the right logic. First, we analyze the project's case. But if it's a new project, then it should be copied immediately. It's clear, but if we have a case, a legacy code without a framework, then of course we need to run the analysis before we copy the templates, because in theory, after the analysis, these templates must be corrected. And even more so, if we meet a case with the previous version of the framework, again, we need to run the analysis first, and then... because in this case, the framework files are not even copied, but rather corrected, and only if necessary.

### üë§ **User** *(10.12.2025, 00:04)*

I think you expressed the right idea that the version of the file "cloud_markdown" should be completely different for the migration stage and for the standard functioning of the framework. And I think it would be right. Because it turns out that we are copying a single version of the cloud file, which is largely intended for migration management. Although, in fact, the need for this is only once. And we need to separate these two stages - the migration stage and the regular functioning stage. And, accordingly, the logic of migration is always, well, of course, first some version of the Markdown code is copied specifically for migration, it is launched. This logic, including our sub-agents, analyzes all the cases, all the files, then it copies all the files, templates, corrects what is needed. And when the migration ends correctly, the final point is the removal of the old version of the code and replacing it with a version that is necessary for the standard framework of its usual functioning without migration. What do you think about this?

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(10.12.2025, 00:04)*

**–î–≤–∞ CLAUDE.md:**

   ‚Üí –°–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å: "Continue from step X or restart?"

   ‚Üí –í—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å swap –Ω–∞ production

```

**migration-log.json:**
```json
{
  "status": "in_progress|completed|failed",
  "mode": "legacy|upgrade",
  "started": "2025-12-10T...",
  "current_step": 3,
  "steps_completed": ["discovery", "analysis", "questions"],
  "last_error": null
}
```

**–ü—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å –º–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏:**
- –ü–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–º —à–∞–≥–æ–º: –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å `current_step` –≤ –ª–æ–≥–µ
- –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ–≥–æ —à–∞–≥–∞: –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –≤ `steps_completed`

## –ü–ª–∞–Ω v2.2.0 ‚Äî –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—ë–Ω–Ω—ã–π

### –ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –¥–≤—É—Ö CLAUDE.md + Migration Recovery

---

### 1. CLAUDE.migration.md

```markdown
# CLAUDE.md ‚Äî Migration Mode

## Step 0: Migration Recovery Check

```bash
cat .claude/migration-log.json 2>/dev/null
```

**–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ñ–∞–π–ª —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç:**

- `status: "in_progress"` ‚Üí –ü—Ä–µ–¥—ã–¥—É—â–∞—è –º–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–µ—Ä–≤–∞–ª–∞—Å—å
  ```
  ‚ö†Ô∏è Migration interrupted at step: [current_step]
  Completed: [steps_completed]
  
  Options:
  1. Continue from step [X]
  2. Restart migration from beginning
  3. Cancel and keep current state
  ```
  
- `status: "completed"` ‚Üí –ú–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∞, –Ω–æ swap –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–æ—à—ë–ª
  ‚Üí –ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å swap –Ω–∞ production
  ‚Üí –£–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å migration-log.json

- `status: "failed"` ‚Üí –ü–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å –æ—à–∏–±–∫—É, —Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å

**–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ –Ω–µ—Ç:**
‚Üí –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å migration-context.json ‚Üí –Ω–∞—á–∞—Ç—å –º–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é

## Step 1: Start Migration

–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å migration-log.json:
```json
{
  "status": "in_progress",
  "mode": "legacy|upgrade", 
  "started": "ISO timestamp",
  "current_step": 1,
  "steps_completed": [],
  "last_error": null
}
```

## –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–≥–æ —à–∞–≥–∞:

```bash
# Update log before step
echo '{"status":"in_progress","current_step":N,...}' > .claude/migration-log.json

# Execute step...

# Update log after success
# Add step name to steps_completed
```

## Final Step: Complete Migration

```bash
# Mark completed
echo '{"status":"completed",...}' > .claude/migration-log.json

# Swap CLAUDE.md
cp .claude/CLAUDE.production.md CLAUDE.md

# Cleanup
rm .claude/CLAUDE.production.md
rm .claude/migration-log.json
rm .claude/migration-context.json
```
```

---

### 2. migration-log.json —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞

```json
{
  "status": "in_progress | completed | failed",
  "mode": "legacy | upgrade",
  "old_version": "v1.x",           // —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–ª—è upgrade
  "started": "2025-12-10T10:30:00",
  "updated": "2025-12-10T10:35:00",
  "current_step": 3,
  "current_step_name": "analysis",
  "steps_completed": [
    {"step": 1, "name": "discovery", "completed": "..."},
    {"step": 2, "name": "questions", "completed": "..."}
  ],
  "last_error": null
}
```

### 5. Recovery —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–∏

**–ü—Ä–µ—Ä–≤–∞–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ step 1-2 (discovery/analysis):**
‚Üí –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ –±–µ–∑–æ–ø–∞—Å–Ω–æ restart ‚Äî –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–æ

**–ü—Ä–µ—Ä–≤–∞–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ step 3-4 (questions/report):**
‚Üí –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ continue ‚Äî –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—ë–Ω –≤ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ Claude
‚Üí –ò–ª–∏ restart

**–ü—Ä–µ—Ä–≤–∞–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ step 5-6 (generate/install):**
‚Üí –ß–∞—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω—ã —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã
‚Üí –ü–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å —á—Ç–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–æ, —Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å: continue –∏–ª–∏ cleanup + restart

**BUG 8: Template Unpacking Order Logic Error - FULLY FIXED**
- User observed: "when we launch the launcher, it first copies the templates... Then, when we launch the framework, especially in the legacy project, it starts the analysis and immediately finds familiar files, which are actually templates that we just unpacked"
- User clarified: "It's just a mistake in logic. Because, as I understand it, the unpacking of all these templates should take place after the project analysis, not before."
- **Root cause:** `init-project.sh` copies ALL files unconditionally before Claude can analyze the original project
- **Impact:** Claude's legacy migration analysis is polluted by template files
- **User confirmed correct approach:**
  - New project: Copy everything immediately
  - Legacy/Upgrade: Copy minimum ‚Üí analyze clean project ‚Üí then create/copy files
- **Fix applied to `init-project.sh` lines 268-347:**
  - Mode check: `if [ "$MIGRATION_MODE" = "new" ]` vs `else` (legacy/upgrade)
  - New: Full copy + template generation (lines 274-325)
  - Legacy/Upgrade: Only `migrate-legacy.md`, `upgrade-framework.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, and `framework-pending.tar.gz` (lines 327-346)
- **Step 7.5 added to `/migrate-legacy.md`** (lines 497-528) - extracts framework-pending.tar.gz after analysis
- **Step 6.5 added to `/upgrade-framework.md`** (lines 473-500) - extracts framework-pending.tar.gz after migration
- **Distribution rebuilt and GitHub Release updated**
- **COMMITTED:** `1737fcf` - pushed to origin, GitHub Release updated

**BUG 5: Dialog UI/Export invocation issue - FULLY FIXED AND DEPLOYED**
- User completed full installation on ChatOpenAII_1 (fresh project)
- Error: `npm error Missing script: "dialog:ui"` when running `/ui` command

**VERIFIED: Files ARE installed correctly:**
```bash
ls -la /Users/alexeykrolmini/Downloads/Code/ChatOpenAII_1/.claude/dist/claude-export/
# Shows: cli.js (13KB), server.js (18KB), exporter.js (32KB), watcher.js (19KB), gitignore.js (8KB), public/
```

**ROOT CAUSE:** Wrong paths in `.claude/commands/ui.md`, `watch.md`, and `fi.md`:
- Commands tried: `npm run dialog:*` (requires npm scripts - won't exist in user's package.json)
- Wrong fallback paths: `node .claude-export/dist/cli.js` (wrong directory structure)
- Correct path: `node .claude/dist/claude-export/cli.js <command>`

**User directive:** "I, as a user, expect that if I downloaded Framework 2 and created a command /ui, then everything should work. Why doesn't it work? Your task is to find out. If you found the reason, you just need to fix it."

**ALL FIXES APPLIED AND DEPLOYED:**

1. `.claude/commands/ui.md` - simplified to use direct node invocation:
   `node .claude/dist/claude-export/cli.js ui`

2. `.claude/commands/watch.md` - simplified to use direct node invocation:
   `node .claude/dist/claude-export/cli.js watch`

3. `.claude/commands/fi.md` line 18 - changed `npm run dialog:export` to:
   `node .claude/dist/claude-export/cli.js export`

4. Rebuilt `dist-release/framework.tar.gz` with `bash migration/build-distribution.sh`

5. Updated GitHub Release: `gh release upload v2.1.1 dist-release/framework.tar.gz --clobber`

6. Committed as `f9a1823`: "fix: Correct CLI paths in slash commands"

**BUG 2: sed escaping error - FIXED LOCALLY, BUT PUSH INCOMPLETE**
Error: `sed: 1: "s/{{CURRENT_BRANCH}}/HE ...": unescaped newline inside substitute pattern`

**Fix applied to `migration/init-project.sh:299`:**
```bash
BRANCH=$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD 2>/dev/null | tr -d '\n' || echo "main")
[ -z "$BRANCH" ] && BRANCH="main"
```

- Local: `267dda608bb2c43d144ed1f8f3252b56`

**BUG 3: Premature "–ì–æ—Ç–æ–≤–æ" claims - PATTERN DETECTED**
User asked "–¢—ã —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ —É–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω?" after I said "–ì–æ—Ç–æ–≤–æ" - prompting verification which found the MD5 mismatch. Need to ALWAYS verify with checksums before claiming done.

**BUG 4: MD5 MISMATCH DESPITE CLEAN GIT STATUS - RESOLVED**
After commit d8025a3 pushed:
- `git status init-project.sh` ‚Üí clean
- `git diff HEAD -- init-project.sh` ‚Üí empty
- Git SHA verified: local `d8025a3df0f0391351447a313f3a48db5189d687` matches GitHub API
- MD5 hashes differed: GitHub raw `a483ef8e...` vs Local `267dda60...`
- raw.githubusercontent.com showed OLD version at line 299 (CDN cached)
- GitHub API showed CORRECT version with fix (bypasses CDN)
- **RESOLUTION:** CDN cache (max-age=300) was serving stale version
- Verified via GitHub blob UI - shows correct fix with HTML encoding
- User challenged CDN explanation, but additional verification confirmed it was correct

**Patterns learned:**
- Don't assume user's workflow - ASK what they actually did
- Don't "hallucinate" context that wasn't discussed
- VERIFY with checksums (MD5) before claiming "ready"
- After push, ALWAYS verify GitHub file matches local with `curl -sL ... | md5` vs `md5 localfile`
- Don't make up technical explanations (like "CDN cache") when you don't fully understand the issue - investigate properly instead

**BUG 6: ES Modules conflict with CommonJS CLI - FIXED (a577908)**
- Error: `ReferenceError: exports is not defined in ES module scope`
- Occurs when host project has `"type": "module"` in package.json (like ChatOpenAII_1)
- CommonJS code in `.claude/dist/claude-export/*.js` fails to load
- **Fix:** Created `dist/claude-export/package.json` with `"type": "commonjs"`
- Rebuilt distribution, updated GitHub Release

**BUG 7: Missing express dependency - FIXED (a577908)**
- Error: `Cannot find module 'express'`
- CLI uses express for web server but doesn't bundle it
- Note: Must use express 4.x, not 5.x (path-to-regexp compatibility issue with `*` syntax)
- **Fix:** Added express dependency to `dist/claude-export/package.json`, updated `/ui` and `/watch` commands with npm install step

# Codebase and System Documentation
_What are the important system components? How do they work/fit together?_

**Framework:** Claude Code Starter v2.0 (meta-framework extending Claude Code)
**Branch:** feat/framework-v2.0

Key protocols:
- **Cold Start Protocol:** migration check ‚Üí crash recovery ‚Üí export dialogs ‚Üí mark active ‚Üí load context
- **Completion Protocol:** build ‚Üí update metafiles ‚Üí export dialogs ‚Üí git commit ‚Üí push/PR ‚Üí mark clean

Session state tracked in `.claude/.last_session` with `"status": "active"` or `"status": "clean"`

# Learnings
_What has worked well? What has not? What to avoid? Do not duplicate items from other sections_

**ARCHITECTURAL INSIGHT - Two-phase CLAUDE.md (v2.2.0):**
- Current CLAUDE.md has migration logic needed only once ‚Üí pollutes normal operation
- Solution: CLAUDE.migration.md (analysis/migration only) ‚Üí swap to CLAUDE.production.md (normal operation)
- User quote: "we need to separate these two stages - the migration stage and the regular functioning stage"
- **Migration Crash Recovery:** Real-time logging to `migration-log.json` enables recovery from interrupted migrations
- Analogous to production Crash Recovery (`.last_session` with `status: active/clean`)

**Template timing is critical:**
- Templates copied before analysis ‚Üí Claude finds templates instead of real project
- Correct flow: copy minimum ‚Üí analyze clean project ‚Üí THEN generate/copy files

**CLI/Commands:**
- Use direct node invocation: `node .claude/dist/claude-export/cli.js <cmd>`
- NOT `npm run dialog:*` (requires npm scripts in user's package.json)
- ES Modules fix: `package.json` with `"type": "commonjs"` must be IN `.claude/dist/claude-export/`
- Express must be 4.x (not 5.x) - path-to-regexp incompatibility

**Distribution hygiene:**
- `/release.md` excluded (dev-only, hardcoded Framework URLs)
- `CLAUDE.template.md` for host projects (no Framework-specific content)
- Single source of truth: `init-project.sh` in root only

**Verification:**
- After push: `git show HEAD:file | md5` vs `md5 localfile`
- GitHub API bypasses CDN cache

**User directives:**
- "–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –≤–Ω–µ—Å–∏ –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏ —Å–∫–∞–∂–∏, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–æ" - just fix, don't ask
- "I don't know. You tell me)))" - when user suspects problem, investigate thoroughly
- When user asks "are you sure?" - VERIFY with checksums
- "I expect that if I downloaded Framework... everything should work" - no excuses

_If the user asked a specific output such as an answer to a question, a table, or other document, repeat the exact result here_

**Final Swap Command (at migration end):**
```bash
# Mark completed
echo '{"status": "completed", "mode": "legacy", "completed": "'$(date -Iseconds)'"}' > .claude/migration-log.json

# Swap CLAUDE.md
cp .claude/CLAUDE.production.md CLAUDE.md
rm .claude/CLAUDE.production.md

# Cleanup
rm .claude/migration-log.json
rm .claude/migration-context.json
```

**VERSION BUMP:** `init-project.sh` line 11: `VERSION="2.2.0"`

**init-project.sh CLAUDE.md Logic Updated (lines 274-353):**
```bash
# NEW mode (line 284-288):
if [ ! -f "CLAUDE.md" ] && [ -f "$TEMP_DIR/framework/CLAUDE.production.md" ]; then
    cp "$TEMP_DIR/framework/CLAUDE.production.md" CLAUDE.md
    log_success "Installed CLAUDE.md (production)"
fi

# LEGACY/UPGRADE mode (lines 338-348):
if [ -f "$TEMP_DIR/framework/CLAUDE.migration.md" ]; then
    cp "$TEMP_DIR/framework/CLAUDE.migration.md" CLAUDE.md
    log_success "Installed CLAUDE.md (migration mode)"
fi
if [ -f "$TEMP_DIR/framework/CLAUDE.production.md" ]; then
    cp "$TEMP_DIR/framework/CLAUDE.production.md" .claude/CLAUDE.production.md
    log_info "Staged CLAUDE.production.md for post-migration swap"
fi
```

# Completion Protocol

Execute the Completion Protocol from `CLAUDE.md`:

1. `npm run build` ‚Äî verify build passes
2. Update metafiles:
   - `.claude/BACKLOG.md` ‚Äî mark completed tasks `[x]`
   - `.claude/SNAPSHOT.md` ‚Äî update version and status
   - `CHANGELOG.md` ‚Äî add entry (if release)
   - `README.md` + `README_RU.md` ‚Äî update if major features added
   - `.claude/ARCHITECTURE.md` ‚Äî update if code structure changed
3. Export dialogs:
   ```bash
   npm run dialog:export
   ```
4. Git commit:
   ```bash
   git add -A && git status
   git commit -m "type: description"
   ```
5. Push & PR check:
   - Ask: "Push to remote?"
   - If yes: `git push`
   - Check: `git log origin/main..HEAD --oneline`
   - If empty ‚Üí All merged, no PR needed
   - If has commits ‚Üí Ask: "Create PR?"
6. Mark session clean:
   ```bash
   echo '{"status": "clean", "timestamp": "'$(date -Iseconds)'"}' > .claude/.last_session
   ```

# Completion Protocol

Execute the Completion Protocol from `CLAUDE.md`:

1. `npm run build` ‚Äî verify build passes
2. Update metafiles:
   - `.claude/BACKLOG.md` ‚Äî mark completed tasks `[x]`
   - `.claude/SNAPSHOT.md` ‚Äî update version and status
   - `CHANGELOG.md` ‚Äî add entry (if release)
   - `README.md` + `README_RU.md` ‚Äî update if major features added
   - `.claude/ARCHITECTURE.md` ‚Äî update if code structure changed
3. Export dialogs:
   ```bash
   npm run dialog:export
   ```
4. Git commit:
   ```bash
   git add -A && git status
   git commit -m "type: description"
   ```
5. Push & PR check:
   - Ask: "Push to remote?"
   - If yes: `git push`
   - Check: `git log origin/main..HEAD --oneline`
   - If empty ‚Üí All merged, no PR needed
   - If has commits ‚Üí Ask: "Create PR?"
6. Mark session clean:
   ```bash
   echo '{"status": "clean", "timestamp": "'$(date -Iseconds)'"}' > .claude/.last_session
   ```
